  <script>
  (function() {
    const data = {{ budget | tojson_safe }};
    const months = data.months;
    const ccys = Object.keys(data.by_currency);

    const ctrl = document.getElementById('budget-ccy-ctrl');
    ccys.forEach(c => {
      const btn = document.createElement('button');
      btn.className = 'ctrl-btn' + (ccys.indexOf(c) === 0 ? ' active' : '');
      btn.textContent = c;
      btn.onclick = function() {
        ctrl.querySelectorAll('.ctrl-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
        this.classList.add('active');
        updateChart(c);
      };
      ctrl.appendChild(btn);
    });

    const ctx = document.getElementById('chart-budget');
    let chart;
    function updateChart(ccy) {
      const d = data.by_currency[ccy];
      if (chart) chart.destroy();
      chart = new Chart(ctx, {
        type: 'bar',
        data: {
          labels: months,
          datasets: [
            { label: 'Actual', data: d.actual, backgroundColor: 'rgba(88,166,255,0.8)' },
            { label: 'Budget', data: d.budget, backgroundColor: 'rgba(139,148,158,0.5)', borderColor: '#8b949e', borderWidth: 1 },
            { label: 'Variance', data: d.variance, type: 'line', borderColor: d.variance.map(v => v >= 0 ? '#3fb950' : '#f85149'), backgroundColor: 'transparent', borderWidth: 2, pointRadius: 3 },
          ]
        },
        options: {
          responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false,
          plugins: { legend: { labels: { color: '#e6edf3', font: { size: 11 } } } },
          scales: {
            x: { ticks: { color: '#8b949e', maxRotation: 45, font: { size: 10 } } },
            y: { ticks: { color: '#8b949e' } }
          }
        }
      });
    }
    if (ccys.length) updateChart(ccys[0]);
  })();
  </script>

  {% else %}
  <div style="text-align: center; padding: 60px; color: var(--text-secondary);">
    <p>No budget data available.</p>
    <p style="font-size: 0.85rem;">Provide budget.xlsx with monthly NII targets per currency.</p>

<div id="tab-coc" class="tab-content">
  <h3 style="font-size: 0.9rem; margin-bottom: 12px;">Cost of Carry Decomposition</h3>

  {% if has_coc %}
  <!-- Controls -->
  <div class="controls">
    <span style="color: var(--text-secondary); font-size: 0.8rem; line-height: 32px; margin-right: 8px;">Currency:</span>
    <button class="ctrl-btn active" onclick="setCocCurrency('All')">All</button>
    <button class="ctrl-btn" onclick="setCocCurrency('CHF')">CHF</button>
    <button class="ctrl-btn" onclick="setCocCurrency('EUR')">EUR</button>
    <button class="ctrl-btn" onclick="setCocCurrency('USD')">USD</button>
    <button class="ctrl-btn" onclick="setCocCurrency('GBP')">GBP</button>
    <span style="width: 16px;"></span>
    <span style="color: var(--text-secondary); font-size: 0.8rem; line-height: 32px; margin-right: 8px;">Shock:</span>
    <button class="ctrl-btn active" onclick="setCocShock('shock_0')">Base</button>
    <button class="ctrl-btn" onclick="setCocShock('shock_50')">+50bp</button>
    <button class="ctrl-btn" onclick="setCocShock('shock_wirp')">WIRP</button>
  </div>

  <!-- Chart -->
  <div class="card">
    <div class="chart-container">
      <canvas id="chart-coc"></canvas>
    </div>
    <p class="footnote">
      P&amp;L Simple = FundingCost &minus; GrossCarry (OIS forward, linear).
      P&amp;L Compounded = Nom &times; [&prod;(1+f&middot;d/D) &minus; &prod;(1+r&middot;d/D)] (WASP carry, geometric).
    </p>

  <script>
  (function() {
    const cocData = {{ coc | tojson_safe }};
    let cocCurrency = 'All';
    let cocShock = 'shock_0';
    let cocChart = null;

    function renderCocChart() {
      const ctx = document.getElementById('chart-coc');
      if (!ctx || typeof Chart === 'undefined' || !cocData.months.length) return;
      if (cocChart) cocChart.destroy();

      const ccy = cocData.by_currency[cocCurrency] || {};
      const shock = ccy[cocShock] || {};
      const gc = shock.GrossCarry || [];
      const fc = shock.FundingCost_Simple || [];
      const cs = shock.PnL_Simple || [];
      const cc = shock.PnL_Compounded || [];

      cocChart = new Chart(ctx, {
        type: 'bar',
        data: {
          labels: cocData.months,
          datasets: [
            {
              label: 'GrossCarry',
              data: gc,
              backgroundColor: 'rgba(63, 185, 80, 0.6)',
              borderColor: '#3fb950',
              borderWidth: 1,
              order: 2,
            },
            {
              label: 'Funding (Fwd)',
              data: fc.map(v => -Math.abs(v)),
              backgroundColor: 'rgba(248, 81, 73, 0.6)',
              borderColor: '#f85149',
              borderWidth: 1,
              order: 2,
            },
            {
              label: 'P&L Simple',
              data: cs,
              type: 'line',
              borderColor: '#58a6ff',
              backgroundColor: 'transparent',
              borderWidth: 2,
              pointRadius: 0,
              tension: 0.3,
              order: 1,
            },
            {
              label: 'P&L Compounded',
              data: cc,
              type: 'line',
              borderColor: '#58a6ff',
              borderDash: [6, 3],
              backgroundColor: 'transparent',
              borderWidth: 2,
              pointRadius: 0,
              tension: 0.3,
              order: 1,
            },
          ]
        },
        options: {
          responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false,
          interaction: { mode: 'index', intersect: false },
          plugins: { legend: { labels: { color: '#e6edf3', font: { size: 11 } } } },
          scales: {
            x: { ticks: { color: '#8b949e', maxRotation: 45, font: { size: 10 } } },
            y: { ticks: { color: '#8b949e' } }
          }
        }
      });
    }

    window.setCocCurrency = function(ccy) {
      cocCurrency = ccy;
      document.querySelectorAll('#tab-coc .controls .ctrl-btn').forEach(b => {
        if (b.textContent.trim() === ccy) b.classList.add('active');
        else if (['All','CHF','EUR','USD','GBP'].includes(b.textContent.trim())) {
          if (b.textContent.trim() !== ccy) b.classList.remove('active');
        }
      });
      renderCocChart();
    };

    window.setCocShock = function(shock) {
      cocShock = shock;
      const labels = {'shock_0':'Base','shock_50':'+50bp','shock_wirp':'WIRP'};
      document.querySelectorAll('#tab-coc .controls .ctrl-btn').forEach(b => {
        const t = b.textContent.trim();
        if (labels[shock] === t) b.classList.add('active');
        else if (['Base','+50bp','WIRP'].includes(t) && labels[shock] !== t) b.classList.remove('active');
      });
      renderCocChart();
    };

    renderCocChart();
  })();
  </script>

  {% else %}
  <div style="text-align: center; padding: 60px; color: var(--text-secondary);">
    <p>No Cost of Carry data available.</p>
    <p style="font-size: 0.85rem;">Ensure <code>funding_source</code> is configured and CoC measures are computed.</p>
  </div>
  {% endif %}

  <script>
  (function() {
    const top10 = {{ counterparty_pnl.top_10 | tojson_safe }};

    // Horizontal bar — top counterparties
    const ctxBar = document.getElementById('chart-cpty-bar');

        type: 'bar',

          labels: top10.map(r => r.counterparty),
          datasets: [{
            data: top10.map(r => r.pnl),
            backgroundColor: top10.map(r => r.pnl >= 0 ? 'rgba(63,185,80,0.7)' : 'rgba(248,81,73,0.7)'),
          }]
        },
        options: {
          indexAxis: 'y', responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false,
          plugins: { legend: { display: false } },
          scales: {
            x: { ticks: { color: '#8b949e' } },
            y: { ticks: { color: '#e6edf3', font: { size: 10 } } }
          }
        }
      });
    }

    // Donut — product breakdown
    const ctxProd = document.getElementById('chart-cpty-product');
    if (ctxProd && typeof Chart !== 'undefined') {
      const prods = Object.keys(byProduct);
      new Chart(ctxProd, {
        type: 'doughnut',
        data: {
          labels: prods,
          datasets: [{
            data: prods.map(p => Math.abs(byProduct[p].value)),
            backgroundColor: prods.map(p => byProduct[p].color),
          }]
        },
        options: {
          responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false,
          plugins: { legend: { labels: { color: '#e6edf3', font: { size: 11 } } } }
        }
      });
    }
  })();
  </script>

  <div style="text-align: center; padding: 60px; color: var(--text-secondary);">
    <p>No counterparty P&amp;L data available.</p>
    <p style="font-size: 0.85rem;">Counterparty metadata is required in deal data.</p>

===FILE START=== src/cockpit/pnl_dashboard/templates/_currency_mismatch.html
<div id="tab-currency-mismatch" class="tab-content">
  <h3 style="font-size: 0.9rem; margin-bottom: 12px;">Currency Mismatch &mdash; Assets vs Liabilities</h3>

  {% if has_currency_mismatch %}
  <div class="controls" id="mismatch-ccy-ctrl"></div>

  <div class="card">
    <div class="chart-container">
      <canvas id="chart-mismatch"></canvas>
    </div>
  </div>

  <div class="card">
    <h3 style="font-size: 0.85rem; margin-bottom: 8px;">Net Gap by Currency</h3>
    <div style="overflow-x: auto;">
    <table id="tbl-mismatch">
      <thead><tr><th>Month</th>
      {% for ccy in currency_mismatch.by_currency.keys() %}
        {% if ccy != "All" %}<th>{{ ccy }}</th>{% endif %}
      {% endfor %}
      <th>Total</th></tr></thead>
      <tbody></tbody>
    </table>
    </div>
  </div>

  <script>
  (function() {
    const data = {{ currency_mismatch | tojson_safe }};
    const months = data.months;

    // Currency selector
    const ctrl = document.getElementById('mismatch-ccy-ctrl');
    const ccys = Object.keys(data.by_currency);
    ccys.forEach(c => {
      const btn = document.createElement('button');
      btn.className = 'ctrl-btn' + (c === 'All' ? ' active' : '');
      btn.textContent = c;
      btn.onclick = function() {
        ctrl.querySelectorAll('.ctrl-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
        this.classList.add('active');
        updateChart(c);
      };
      ctrl.appendChild(btn);
    });

    const ctx = document.getElementById('chart-mismatch');
    if (!ctx || typeof Chart === 'undefined') return;

    let chart;
    function updateChart(ccy) {
      const d = data.by_currency[ccy];
      if (chart) chart.destroy();
      chart = new Chart(ctx, {
        type: 'bar',
        data: {
          labels: months,
          datasets: [
            { label: 'Assets', data: d.assets, backgroundColor: 'rgba(63,185,80,0.7)', stack: 'stack' },
            { label: 'Liabilities', data: d.liabilities.map(v => -Math.abs(v)), backgroundColor: 'rgba(248,81,73,0.7)', stack: 'stack' },
            { label: 'Gap', data: d.gap, type: 'line', borderColor: '#58a6ff', backgroundColor: 'transparent', borderWidth: 2, pointRadius: 2, yAxisID: 'y' },
          ]
        },
        options: {
          responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false,
          plugins: { legend: { labels: { color: '#e6edf3', font: { size: 11 } } } },
          scales: {
            x: { ticks: { color: '#8b949e', maxRotation: 45, font: { size: 10 } } },
            y: { ticks: { color: '#8b949e' } }
          }
        }
      });
    }
    updateChart('All');

    // Table
    const tbody = document.querySelector('#tbl-mismatch tbody');
    const ccyList = ccys.filter(c => c !== 'All');
    months.forEach((m, i) => {
      let row = '<tr><td>' + m + '</td>';
      ccyList.forEach(c => {
        const g = data.by_currency[c].gap[i];
        row += '<td class="' + valClass(g) + '">' + fmt(g) + '</td>';
      });
      const tot = data.by_currency['All'] ? data.by_currency['All'].gap[i] : 0;
      row += '<td class="' + valClass(tot) + '"><strong>' + fmt(tot) + '</strong></td></tr>';
      tbody.innerHTML += row;
    });
  })();
  </script>

  <!-- Basis Risk: Cross-Currency OIS Spread -->
  {% if currency_mismatch.basis_risk %}
  <div class="card" style="margin-top: 16px;">
    <h3 style="font-size: 0.85rem; margin-bottom: 8px;">Basis Risk &mdash; Cross-Currency OIS Spread (bps)</h3>
    <div class="chart-container chart-sm">
      <canvas id="chart-basis-risk"></canvas>
    </div>
    <p class="footnote">OIS forward rate spread vs CHF. Widening spread = increased cross-currency funding cost.</p>
  </div>
  <script>
  (function() {
    const basis = {{ currency_mismatch.basis_risk | tojson_safe }};
    const months = {{ currency_mismatch.months | tojson_safe }};
    const ctx = document.getElementById('chart-basis-risk');
    if (!ctx || typeof Chart === 'undefined' || !Object.keys(basis).length) return;
    const datasets = [];
    for (const [pair, d] of Object.entries(basis)) {
      datasets.push({
        label: pair,
        data: d.values,
        borderColor: d.color,
        backgroundColor: 'transparent',
        borderWidth: 2,
        pointRadius: 2,
        tension: 0.3,
      });
    }
    new Chart(ctx, {
      type: 'line',
      data: { labels: months, datasets: datasets },
      options: {
        responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false,
        plugins: { legend: { labels: { color: '#e6edf3' } } },
        scales: {
          x: { ticks: { color: '#8b949e', maxRotation: 45 } },
          y: { title: { display: true, text: 'Spread (bps)', color: '#8b949e' }, ticks: { color: '#8b949e' }, grid: { color: '#21262d' } }
        }
      }
    });
  })();
  </script>
  {% endif %}

  {% else %}
  <div style="text-align: center; padding: 60px; color: var(--text-secondary);">
    <p>No currency mismatch data available.</p>
  </div>
  {% endif %}
</div>

===FILE START=== src/cockpit/pnl_dashboard/templates/_curves.html
<div id="tab-curves" class="tab-content">
  <h3 style="font-size: 0.9rem; margin-bottom: 12px;">OIS Forward Curves</h3>

  {% if has_curves %}
  <div class="card">
    <div class="chart-container">
      <canvas id="chart-curves"></canvas>
    </div>
  </div>

  <!-- WIRP meeting points -->
  {% if curves.wirp_points %}
  <div class="card">
    <h3 style="font-size: 0.85rem; margin-bottom: 8px;">WIRP Meeting Expectations</h3>
    <div style="overflow-x: auto;">
    <table>
      <thead><tr><th>Date</th><th>Currency</th><th>Expected Rate (%)</th></tr></thead>
      <tbody>
      {% for pt in curves.wirp_points %}
        <tr><td>{{ pt.date }}</td><td>{{ pt.currency }}</td><td>{{ "{:.4f}".format(pt.rate) }}</td></tr>
      {% endfor %}
      </tbody>
    </table>
    </div>
  </div>
  {% endif %}

  <script>
  (function() {
    const curvesData = {{ curves.series | tojson_safe }};
    const ctx = document.getElementById('chart-curves');
    if (!ctx || typeof Chart === 'undefined') return;

    const datasets = [];
    for (const [ccy, series] of Object.entries(curvesData)) {
      datasets.push({
        label: ccy + ' OIS',
        data: series.dates.map((d, i) => ({ x: d, y: series.values[i] })),
        borderColor: series.color,
        backgroundColor: 'transparent',
        borderWidth: 2,
        pointRadius: 0,
        tension: 0.3,
      });
    }

    // WIRP scatter overlay
    const wirpPoints = {{ curves.wirp_points | tojson_safe }};
    const wirpColors = { CHF: '#d62828', EUR: '#e67e22', USD: '#002868', GBP: '#6f42c1' };
    if (wirpPoints && wirpPoints.length) {
      const byCcy = {};
      wirpPoints.forEach(pt => {
        if (!byCcy[pt.currency]) byCcy[pt.currency] = [];
        byCcy[pt.currency].push({ x: pt.date, y: pt.rate });
      });
      for (const [ccy, pts] of Object.entries(byCcy)) {
        datasets.push({
          label: ccy + ' WIRP',
          data: pts,
          type: 'scatter',
          backgroundColor: wirpColors[ccy] || '#8b949e',
          borderColor: wirpColors[ccy] || '#8b949e',
          pointRadius: 5,
          pointStyle: 'triangle',
        });
      }
    }

    new Chart(ctx, {
      type: 'line',
      data: { datasets },
      options: {
        responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false,
        interaction: { mode: 'index', intersect: false },
        plugins: { legend: { labels: { color: '#e6edf3', font: { size: 11 } } } },
        scales: {
          x: { type: 'category', ticks: { color: '#8b949e', maxRotation: 45, font: { size: 10 } } },
          y: { ticks: { color: '#8b949e' }, title: { display: true, text: 'Rate (%)', color: '#8b949e' } }
        }
      }
    });
  })();
  </script>

  {% else %}
  <div style="text-align: center; padding: 60px; color: var(--text-secondary);">
    <p>No rate curve data available.</p>
    <p style="font-size: 0.85rem;">OIS forward curves are required for this view.</p>
  </div>
  {% endif %}
</div>

    function filterTable() {
      const search = (searchEl.value || '').toLowerCase();
      const ccy = ccyEl.value;
      const prod = prodEl.value;
      const sign = signEl.value;
      table.querySelectorAll('tbody tr').forEach(function(row) {
        const text = row.textContent.toLowerCase();
        const rCcy = row.dataset.ccy;
        const rProd = row.dataset.product;
        const rPnl = parseFloat(row.dataset.pnl || 0);
        let show = true;
        if (search && text.indexOf(search) === -1) show = false;
        if (ccy && rCcy !== ccy) show = false;
        if (prod && rProd !== prod) show = false;
        if (sign === 'positive' && rPnl <= 0) show = false;
        if (sign === 'negative' && rPnl > 0) show = false;
        row.style.display = show ? '' : 'none';
      });
    }
    if (searchEl) searchEl.addEventListener('input', filterTable);
    if (ccyEl) ccyEl.addEventListener('change', filterTable);
    if (prodEl) prodEl.addEventListener('change', filterTable);
    if (signEl) signEl.addEventListener('change', filterTable);
  })();

  // Column sorting
  var dealSortDir = {};
  function sortDealTable(colIdx) {
    var table = document.getElementById('deal-explorer-table');
    var rows = Array.from(table.querySelectorAll('tbody tr'));
    var dir = dealSortDir[colIdx] === 'asc' ? 'desc' : 'asc';
    dealSortDir[colIdx] = dir;
    rows.sort(function(a, b) {
      var av = a.cells[colIdx].textContent.replace(/[,\s+]/g, '');
      var bv = b.cells[colIdx].textContent.replace(/[,\s+]/g, '');
      var an = parseFloat(av), bn = parseFloat(bv);
      if (!isNaN(an) && !isNaN(bn)) return dir === 'asc' ? an - bn : bn - an;
      return dir === 'asc' ? av.localeCompare(bv) : bv.localeCompare(av);
    });
    var tbody = table.querySelector('tbody');
    rows.forEach(function(r) { tbody.appendChild(r); });
  }
  </script>

  {% else %}
  <div style="text-align: center; padding: 60px; color: var(--text-secondary);">
    <p>No deal-level data available.</p>
    <p style="font-size: 0.85rem;">Provide pnl_by_deal from the P&amp;L engine to enable the Deal Explorer.</p>
  </div>
  {% endif %}
</div>

<script>
(function() {
  // Duration bar chart
  {% if eve.duration and eve.duration.labels %}
  new Chart(document.getElementById('eveDurationChart'), {
    type: 'bar',
    data: {
      labels: {{ eve.duration.labels | tojson_safe }},
      datasets: [{

    Shows how the 12-month forward NII forecast has evolved over time.
    Stable forecasts indicate consistent rate positioning.
    High revision volatility suggests model sensitivity to market moves or portfolio changes.
  </p>

  <script>
  (function() {
    const data = {{ forecast_tracking | tojson_safe }};
    const ctx = document.getElementById('chart-forecast-tracking');
    if (!ctx || typeof Chart === 'undefined') return;

    const datasets = [];
    const colors = { CHF: '#d62828', EUR: '#e67e22', USD: '#002868', GBP: '#6f42c1' };

    for (const [ccy, values] of Object.entries(data.by_currency)) {
      datasets.push({
        label: ccy,
        data: values,
        borderColor: colors[ccy] || '#8b949e',
        backgroundColor: 'transparent',
        borderWidth: 2,
        pointRadius: 2,
        tension: 0.3,
      });
    }
    datasets.push({
      label: 'Total',
      data: data.total,
      borderColor: '#58a6ff',
      backgroundColor: 'transparent',
      borderWidth: 3,
      borderDash: [5, 3],
      pointRadius: 2,
      tension: 0.3,
    });

    new Chart(ctx, {
      type: 'line',
      data: { labels: data.dates, datasets },
      options: {
        responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false,
        interaction: { mode: 'index', intersect: false },
        plugins: { legend: { labels: { color: '#e6edf3', font: { size: 11 } } } },
        scales: {
          x: { ticks: { color: '#8b949e', maxRotation: 45, font: { size: 10 } } },
          y: { ticks: { color: '#8b949e' }, title: { display: true, text: '12M NII Forecast', color: '#8b949e' } }
        }
      }
    });

    // Revision bars
    var revCtx = document.getElementById('chart-forecast-revisions');
    if (revCtx && data.revisions && data.revisions.dates && data.revisions.dates.length) {
      new Chart(revCtx, {
        type: 'bar',
        data: {
          labels: data.revisions.dates,
          datasets: [{
            label: 'Revision',
            data: data.revisions.changes,
            backgroundColor: data.revisions.changes.map(v => v >= 0 ? 'rgba(63,185,80,0.7)' : 'rgba(248,81,73,0.7)'),
            borderWidth: 0,
          }]
        },
        options: {
          responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false,
          plugins: { legend: { display: false } },
          scales: {
            x: { ticks: { color: '#8b949e', maxRotation: 45, font: { size: 9 } } },
            y: { ticks: { color: '#8b949e' }, title: { display: true, text: 'Revision (abs)', color: '#8b949e' } }
          }
        }
      });
    }

    // Revision % bars
    var revPctCtx = document.getElementById('chart-forecast-revisions-pct');
    if (revPctCtx && data.revisions && data.revisions.dates && data.revisions.dates.length) {
      new Chart(revPctCtx, {
        type: 'bar',
        data: {
          labels: data.revisions.dates,
          datasets: [{
            label: 'Revision %',
            data: data.revisions.pct_changes,
            backgroundColor: data.revisions.pct_changes.map(v => v >= 0 ? 'rgba(63,185,80,0.7)' : 'rgba(248,81,73,0.7)'),
            borderWidth: 0,
          }]
        },
        options: {
          responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false,
          plugins: { legend: { display: false } },
          scales: {
            x: { ticks: { color: '#8b949e', maxRotation: 45, font: { size: 9 } } },
            y: { ticks: { color: '#8b949e', callback: function(v) { return v + '%'; } }, title: { display: true, text: 'Revision %', color: '#8b949e' } }
          }
        }
      });
    }
  })();
  </script>

          <td>{{ "{:.4f}".format(p.dollar_offset) }}</td>
          <td>{{ "{:.4f}".format(p.r_squared) }}</td>
          <td>{{ "{:,.0f}".format(p.hedged_pnl) }}</td>
          <td>{{ "{:,.0f}".format(p.instrument_pnl) }}</td>
          <td>
            {% if p.status == 'pass' %}
            <span style="color: var(--accent-green); font-weight: 600;">PASS</span>
            {% else %}
            <span style="color: var(--accent-red); font-weight: 600;">FAIL</span>
            {% endif %}
          </td>
        </tr>
      {% endfor %}
      </tbody>
    </table>
    </div>
  </div>

  <!-- Scenario Cross-Reference -->
  {% if hedge.scenario_xref %}
  <div class="card" style="margin-top: 16px;">
    <h3 style="font-size: 0.85rem; margin-bottom: 8px;">Hedge Performance Under Stress Scenarios</h3>

    </div>

        </tr>
      {% endfor %}
      </tbody>
    </table>
    <p class="footnote">If maturing assets are reinvested at current OIS forward rate. Positive spread = reinvestment at higher rate (NII gain).</p>
  </div>
  {% endif %}

  <p class="footnote">Inflows (green) = maturing assets. Outflows (red) = maturing liabilities. Blue line = cumulative net position.</p>

  <script>
  (function() {
    const data = {{ liquidity | tojson_safe }};
    const ccys = data.all_currencies || Object.keys(data.by_currency);

    // Build "All" aggregate
    const allCcys = Object.keys(data.by_currency);
    if (allCcys.length > 0) {
      const first = data.by_currency[allCcys[0]];
      const allData = {
        labels: first.labels,
        inflows: first.labels.map(() => 0),
        outflows: first.labels.map(() => 0),
        net: first.labels.map(() => 0),
        cumulative: [],
      };
      allCcys.forEach(c => {
        const d = data.by_currency[c];
        for (let i = 0; i < d.inflows.length; i++) {
          allData.inflows[i] += d.inflows[i];
          allData.outflows[i] += d.outflows[i];
          allData.net[i] += d.net[i];
        }
      });
      let cum = 0;
      allData.net.forEach(n => { cum += n; allData.cumulative.push(cum); });
      data.by_currency['All'] = allData;
    }

    const ctrl = document.getElementById('liq-ccy-ctrl');
    const allBtns = ['All'].concat(ccys);
    allBtns.forEach((c, i) => {
      const btn = document.createElement('button');
      btn.className = 'ctrl-btn' + (i === 0 ? ' active' : '');
      btn.textContent = c;
      btn.onclick = function() {
        ctrl.querySelectorAll('.ctrl-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
        this.classList.add('active');
        updateChart(c);
      };
      ctrl.appendChild(btn);
    });

    const ctx = document.getElementById('chart-liquidity');
    let chart;
    function updateChart(ccy) {
      const d = data.by_currency[ccy];
      if (!d) return;
      if (chart) chart.destroy();

      // Thin down labels for readability: show every Nth label
      const step = d.labels.length > 30 ? Math.ceil(d.labels.length / 30) : 1;
      const displayLabels = d.labels.map((l, i) => i % step === 0 ? l : '');

      chart = new Chart(ctx, {
        type: 'bar',
        data: {
          labels: displayLabels,
          datasets: [
            {
              label: 'Inflows',
              data: d.inflows,
              backgroundColor: 'rgba(63,185,80,0.7)',
              stack: 'cashflow',
            },
            {
              label: 'Outflows',
              data: d.outflows,
              backgroundColor: 'rgba(248,81,73,0.7)',
              stack: 'cashflow',
            },
            {
              label: 'Cumulative Net',
              data: d.cumulative,
              type: 'line',
              borderColor: '#58a6ff',
              backgroundColor: 'transparent',
              borderWidth: 2,
              pointRadius: 0,
              yAxisID: 'y1',
            },
          ]
        },
        options: {
          responsive: true,
          maintainAspectRatio: false,
          plugins: {
            legend: { labels: { color: '#e6edf3', font: { size: 11 } } },
            tooltip: { mode: 'index', intersect: false },
          },
          scales: {
            x: { stacked: true, ticks: { color: '#8b949e', maxRotation: 45, font: { size: 9 } } },
            y: { stacked: true, position: 'left', ticks: { color: '#8b949e' }, title: { display: true, text: 'Cash Flow', color: '#8b949e' } },
            y1: { position: 'right', ticks: { color: '#58a6ff' }, title: { display: true, text: 'Cumulative', color: '#58a6ff' }, grid: { drawOnChartArea: false } },
          }
        }
      });
    }
    updateChart('All');
  })();
  </script>

  {% else %}
  <div style="text-align: center; padding: 60px; color: var(--text-secondary);">
    <p>No liquidity schedule data available.</p>
    <p style="font-size: 0.85rem;">Provide liquidity_schedule.xlsx with daily (90d) + monthly cash flow projections per deal.</p>
  </div>
  {% endif %}
</div>

===FILE START=== src/cockpit/pnl_dashboard/templates/_macros.html
{#- Shared Jinja2 macro library for the P&L dashboard.
    Import in any template:  {% from "_macros.html" import kpi_card, chart_container, data_table, metric_badge %}
-#}

{#- KPI card with optional colored left border and sub-label.
    Arguments:
      label       – header text
      value       – main display value (string or number)
      css_class   – extra class on the value div ("positive", "negative", "")
      sub         – optional sub-label text below the value
      border_color – optional left-border color (hex string, e.g. "#f85149")
      id          – optional id for the value div (for JS hydration)
      sub_id      – optional id for the sub div
-#}
{% macro kpi_card(label, value="—", css_class="", sub="", border_color="", id="", sub_id="") %}
<div class="kpi-card"{% if border_color %} style="border-left: 3px solid {{ border_color }};"{% endif %}>
  <div class="kpi-label">{{ label }}</div>
  <div class="kpi-value {{ css_class }}"{% if id %} id="{{ id }}"{% endif %}>{{ value }}</div>
  {% if sub %}<div class="sub"{% if sub_id %} id="{{ sub_id }}"{% endif %}>{{ sub }}</div>{% endif %}
</div>
{% endmacro %}

{#- Chart container: a .card wrapper with a title and a <canvas>.
    Arguments:
      title    – card heading
      chart_id – canvas element id
      height   – canvas height attribute (default 250)
-#}
{% macro chart_container(title, chart_id, height=250) %}
<div class="card">
  <h3>{{ title }}</h3>
  <canvas id="{{ chart_id }}" height="{{ height }}"></canvas>
</div>
{% endmacro %}

{#- Data table with auto-generated <thead> and <tbody>.
    Arguments:
      headers    – list of column header strings
      rows       – list of lists (each inner list = one row's cell values)
      aligns     – optional list of "left"/"right"/"center" per column
      footer_row – optional list (rendered bold with top border)
-#}
{% macro data_table(headers, rows, aligns=none, footer_row=none) %}
<table>
  <thead>
    <tr>
      {% for h in headers %}
      <th{% if aligns and aligns[loop.index0] != "left" %} style="text-align:{{ aligns[loop.index0] }};"{% endif %}>{{ h }}</th>
      {% endfor %}
    </tr>
  </thead>
  <tbody>
    {% for row in rows %}
    <tr>
      {% for cell in row %}
      <td{% if aligns and aligns[loop.index0] != "left" %} style="text-align:{{ aligns[loop.index0] }};"{% endif %}>{{ cell }}</td>
      {% endfor %}
    </tr>
    {% endfor %}
    {% if footer_row %}
    <tr style="font-weight: bold; border-top: 2px solid var(--border);">
      {% for cell in footer_row %}
      <td{% if aligns and aligns[loop.index0] != "left" %} style="text-align:{{ aligns[loop.index0] }};"{% endif %}>{{ cell }}</td>
      {% endfor %}
    </tr>
    {% endif %}
  </tbody>
</table>
{% endmacro %}

{#- Inline severity / metric badge.
    Arguments:
      text      – badge text (e.g. "CRITICAL", "PASS", "FAIL")
      severity  – "critical", "high", "medium", "success", "info"
-#}
{% macro metric_badge(text, severity="info") %}
{%- set colors = {
  "critical": {"bg": "rgba(248,81,73,0.2)", "fg": "var(--accent-red)"},
  "high":     {"bg": "rgba(210,153,34,0.2)", "fg": "var(--accent-yellow)"},
  "medium":   {"bg": "rgba(88,166,255,0.2)", "fg": "var(--accent-blue)"},
  "success":  {"bg": "rgba(63,185,80,0.2)",  "fg": "var(--accent-green)"},
  "info":     {"bg": "rgba(139,148,158,0.2)", "fg": "var(--text-secondary)"},
} -%}
{%- set c = colors.get(severity, colors.info) -%}
<span style="font-size: 0.7rem; text-transform: uppercase; padding: 2px 8px; border-radius: 3px; background: {{ c.bg }}; color: {{ c.fg }};">{{ text }}</span>
{% endmacro %}

{#- Empty-state placeholder when a tab has no data.
    Arguments:
      message – main message text
      hint    – optional smaller hint text
-#}
{% macro empty_state(message, hint="") %}
<div class="card" style="text-align: center; padding: 48px;">
  <p style="color: var(--text-secondary);">{{ message }}</p>
  {% if hint %}<p style="font-size: 0.85rem; color: var(--text-secondary);">{{ hint }}</p>{% endif %}
</div>
{% endmacro %}

          responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false,

          plugins: { legend: { labels: { color: '#e6edf3', font: { size: 11 } } } },
          scales: {
            x: { ticks: { color: '#8b949e' } },
            y: { position: 'left', ticks: { color: '#8b949e' }, title: { display: true, text: 'Rate (bps)', color: '#8b949e' } },
            y1: { position: 'right', grid: { drawOnChartArea: false }, ticks: { color: '#8b949e' }, title: { display: true, text: 'NIM (bps)', color: '#8b949e' } }
          }
        }
      });
    }

    // NIM by currency bar chart
    if (typeof Chart !== 'undefined' && data.by_currency) {
      const ccys = Object.keys(data.by_currency);
      new Chart(document.getElementById('chart-nim-currency'), {
        type: 'bar',

          labels: ccys,

            borderWidth: 0,
          }]
        },
        options: {
          responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false,
          plugins: { legend: { display: false } },
          scales: {
            x: { ticks: { color: '#8b949e' } },
            y: { ticks: { color: '#8b949e' }, title: { display: true, text: 'NIM (bps)', color: '#8b949e' } }
          }
        }
      });
    }

    // NIM by perimeter bar chart
    var periCanvas = document.getElementById('chart-nim-perimeter');
    if (typeof Chart !== 'undefined' && periCanvas && data.by_perimeter) {
      const peris = Object.keys(data.by_perimeter);
      new Chart(periCanvas, {
        type: 'bar',
        data: {
          labels: peris,
          datasets: [{
            label: 'NIM (bps)',
            data: peris.map(p => data.by_perimeter[p].nim_bps),
            backgroundColor: ['rgba(88,166,255,0.8)', 'rgba(63,185,80,0.8)', 'rgba(210,153,34,0.8)', 'rgba(139,148,158,0.8)'],
            borderWidth: 0,
          }]
        },
        options: {
          responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false,
          plugins: { legend: { display: false } },
          scales: {

            y: { ticks: { color: '#8b949e' }, title: { display: true, text: 'NIM (bps)', color: '#8b949e' } }

  })();

            }

        },
        scales: {

        }

    });
  })();

===FILE START=== src/cockpit/pnl_dashboard/templates/_pnl_series.html
<div id="tab-pnl-series" class="tab-content">
  <h3 style="font-size: 0.9rem; margin-bottom: 12px;">P&amp;L Time Series</h3>

  <!-- Shock selector -->
  <div class="controls">
    <span style="color: var(--text-secondary); font-size: 0.8rem; line-height: 32px; margin-right: 8px;">Shock:</span>
    <button class="ctrl-btn active" onclick="setPnlShock('0')">Base</button>
    <button class="ctrl-btn" onclick="setPnlShock('50')">+50bp</button>
    <button class="ctrl-btn" onclick="setPnlShock('wirp')">WIRP</button>
  </div>

  <!-- Main chart: by currency -->
  <div class="card">
    <h3 style="font-size: 0.85rem; margin-bottom: 8px;">Monthly P&amp;L by Currency</h3>
    <div class="chart-container">
      <canvas id="chart-pnl-currency"></canvas>
    </div>
  </div>

  <!-- Product breakdown -->
  <div class="card">
    <h3 style="font-size: 0.85rem; margin-bottom: 8px;">Product Breakdown (Base)</h3>
    <div class="chart-container">
      <canvas id="chart-pnl-product"></canvas>
    </div>
  </div>

  <script>
  (function() {
    const pnlData = {{ pnl_series | tojson_safe }};
    const colors = { CHF: '#d62828', EUR: '#e67e22', USD: '#002868', GBP: '#6f42c1' };
    let currentShock = '0';
    let pnlCurrencyChart = null;
    let pnlProductChart = null;

    function renderCurrencyChart() {
      const ctx = document.getElementById('chart-pnl-currency');
      if (!ctx || typeof Chart === 'undefined' || !pnlData.months.length) return;
      if (pnlCurrencyChart) pnlCurrencyChart.destroy();

      const datasets = [];
      const shockKey = 'shock_' + currentShock;

      for (const [ccy, shocks] of Object.entries(pnlData.by_currency)) {
        // Realized portion (solid)
        const realizedKey = shockKey + '_realized';
        const forecastKey = shockKey + '_forecast';

        if (shocks[realizedKey] && shocks[forecastKey]) {
          datasets.push({
            label: ccy + ' (Realized)',
            data: shocks[realizedKey],
            backgroundColor: colors[ccy] || '#8b949e',
            stack: 'main',
          });
          datasets.push({
            label: ccy + ' (Forecast)',
            data: shocks[forecastKey],
            backgroundColor: (colors[ccy] || '#8b949e') + '66',
            stack: 'main',
          });
        } else {
          datasets.push({
            label: ccy,
            data: shocks[shockKey] || [],
            backgroundColor: colors[ccy] || '#8b949e',
            stack: 'main',
          });
        }
      }

      // Cumulative line
      const cumulative = [];
      let running = 0;
      for (let i = 0; i < pnlData.months.length; i++) {
        let monthTotal = 0;
        for (const shocks of Object.values(pnlData.by_currency)) {
          const vals = shocks['shock_' + currentShock] || [];
          monthTotal += vals[i] || 0;
        }
        running += monthTotal;
        cumulative.push(running);
      }
      datasets.push({
        label: 'Cumulative',
        data: cumulative,
        type: 'line',
        borderColor: '#58a6ff',
        backgroundColor: 'transparent',
        borderWidth: 2,
        pointRadius: 0,
        tension: 0.3,
        yAxisID: 'y1',
      });

      pnlCurrencyChart = new Chart(ctx, {
        type: 'bar',
        data: { labels: pnlData.months, datasets },
        options: {
          responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false,
          interaction: { mode: 'index', intersect: false },
          plugins: {
            legend: { labels: { color: '#e6edf3', font: { size: 10 } } },
            annotation: pnlData.date_rates_month ? {
              annotations: { ratesLine: {
                type: 'line', scaleID: 'x',
                value: pnlData.date_rates_month,
                borderColor: '#d29922', borderDash: [5,3], borderWidth: 1,
                label: { display: true, content: 'Rates', color: '#d29922', font: { size: 10 } }
              }}
            } : undefined,
          },
          scales: {
            x: { stacked: true, ticks: { color: '#8b949e', maxRotation: 45, font: { size: 10 } } },
            y: { stacked: true, ticks: { color: '#8b949e' }, title: { display: true, text: 'P&L', color: '#8b949e' } },
            y1: { position: 'right', grid: { drawOnChartArea: false }, ticks: { color: '#58a6ff' }, title: { display: true, text: 'Cumulative', color: '#58a6ff' } }
          }
        }
      });
    }

    function renderProductChart() {
      const ctx = document.getElementById('chart-pnl-product');
      if (!ctx || typeof Chart === 'undefined' || !pnlData.months.length) return;
      if (pnlProductChart) pnlProductChart.destroy();

      const datasets = [];
      for (const [prod, info] of Object.entries(pnlData.by_product)) {
        datasets.push({
          label: prod,
          data: info.values,
          backgroundColor: info.color,
          stack: 'prod',
        });
      }

      pnlProductChart = new Chart(ctx, {
        type: 'bar',
        data: { labels: pnlData.months, datasets },
        options: {
          responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false,
          plugins: { legend: { labels: { color: '#e6edf3', font: { size: 10 } } } },
          scales: {
            x: { stacked: true, ticks: { color: '#8b949e', maxRotation: 45, font: { size: 10 } } },
            y: { stacked: true, ticks: { color: '#8b949e' } }
          }
        }
      });
    }

    window.setPnlShock = function(shock) {
      currentShock = shock;
      const labels = {'0':'Base','50':'+50bp','wirp':'WIRP'};
      document.querySelectorAll('#tab-pnl-series .controls .ctrl-btn').forEach(b => {
        b.classList.toggle('active', b.textContent.trim() === labels[shock]);
      });
      renderCurrencyChart();
    };

    renderCurrencyChart();
    renderProductChart();
  })();
  </script>
</div>

<div id="tab-repricing-gap" class="tab-content">
  <h3 style="font-size: 0.9rem; margin-bottom: 12px;">Repricing Gap Profile</h3>

  {% if has_repricing_gap %}
  <div class="controls" id="reprice-ccy-ctrl"></div>

  <div class="card">
    <div class="chart-container">
      <canvas id="chart-repricing"></canvas>
    </div>
  </div>

  <div class="card">
    <h3 style="font-size: 0.85rem; margin-bottom: 8px;">Gap Detail</h3>
    <div style="overflow-x: auto;">
    <table id="tbl-repricing">
      <thead><tr><th>Bucket</th><th>Assets</th><th>Liabilities</th><th>Gap</th><th>Cumulative Gap</th></tr></thead>
      <tbody></tbody>
    </table>
    </div>
  </div>

  <p class="footnote">Fixed-rate deals reprice at maturity. Floating-rate deals reprice at next fixing date. Buckets follow Basel IRRBB time bands.</p>

  <script>
  (function() {
    const data = {{ repricing_gap | tojson_safe }};
    const buckets = data.buckets;

    // Currency selector
    const ctrl = document.getElementById('reprice-ccy-ctrl');
    const ccys = Object.keys(data.by_currency);
    ccys.forEach(c => {
      const btn = document.createElement('button');
      btn.className = 'ctrl-btn' + (c === 'All' ? ' active' : '');
      btn.textContent = c;
      btn.onclick = function() {
        ctrl.querySelectorAll('.ctrl-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
        this.classList.add('active');
        updateChart(c);
        updateTable(c);
      };
      ctrl.appendChild(btn);
    });

    const ctx = document.getElementById('chart-repricing');
    if (!ctx || typeof Chart === 'undefined') return;

    let chart;
    function updateChart(ccy) {
      const d = data.by_currency[ccy];
      if (chart) chart.destroy();
      chart = new Chart(ctx, {
        type: 'bar',
        data: {
          labels: buckets,
          datasets: [
            { label: 'Assets', data: d.assets, backgroundColor: 'rgba(63,185,80,0.7)' },
            { label: 'Liabilities', data: d.liabilities.map(v => -Math.abs(v)), backgroundColor: 'rgba(248,81,73,0.7)' },
            { label: 'Cumulative Gap', data: d.cumulative_gap, type: 'line', borderColor: '#58a6ff', backgroundColor: 'transparent', borderWidth: 2, pointRadius: 3, yAxisID: 'y' },
          ]
        },
        options: {
          responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false,
          plugins: { legend: { labels: { color: '#e6edf3', font: { size: 11 } } } },
          scales: {
            x: { ticks: { color: '#8b949e', font: { size: 10 } } },
            y: { ticks: { color: '#8b949e' } }
          }
        }
      });
    }

    function updateTable(ccy) {
      const d = data.by_currency[ccy];
      const tbody = document.querySelector('#tbl-repricing tbody');
      tbody.innerHTML = '';
      buckets.forEach((b, i) => {
        const gap = d.gap[i];
        const cum = d.cumulative_gap[i];
        tbody.innerHTML += '<tr><td>' + b + '</td><td>' + fmt(d.assets[i]) + '</td><td>' + fmt(d.liabilities[i]) + '</td><td class="' + valClass(gap) + '">' + fmt(gap) + '</td><td class="' + valClass(cum) + '">' + fmt(cum) + '</td></tr>';
      });
    }

    updateChart('All');
    updateTable('All');
  })();
  </script>

  {% else %}
  <div style="text-align: center; padding: 60px; color: var(--text-secondary);">
    <p>No repricing gap data available.</p>
    <p style="font-size: 0.85rem;">Deal-level data with maturity dates is required.</p>
  </div>
  {% endif %}
</div>

    Probabilities are indicative weights for expected NII calculation.
  </p>

  <script>
  (function() {
    const data = {{ scenario_studio | tojson_safe }};

    if (typeof Chart !== 'undefined' && data.combined && data.combined.length) {
      const labels = data.combined.map(c => c.scenario);
      const datasets = [
        {
          label: 'ΔNII',
          data: data.combined.map(c => c.delta_nii),
          backgroundColor: data.combined.map(c => c.delta_nii >= 0 ? 'rgba(63,185,80,0.7)' : 'rgba(248,81,73,0.7)'),
          borderColor: data.combined.map(c => c.delta_nii >= 0 ? '#3fb950' : '#f85149'),
          borderWidth: 1,
        }
      ];
      if (data.has_eve) {
        datasets.push({
          label: 'ΔEVE',
          data: data.combined.map(c => c.delta_eve),
          backgroundColor: 'rgba(88,166,255,0.5)',
          borderColor: '#58a6ff',
          borderWidth: 1,
        });
      }
      new Chart(document.getElementById('chart-scenario-combined'), {
        type: 'bar',
        data: { labels: labels, datasets: datasets },
        options: {
          responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false,
          plugins: {
            legend: { labels: { color: '#e6edf3' } },
            title: { display: false }
          },
          scales: {
            x: { ticks: { color: '#8b949e', font: { size: 10 } }, grid: { color: '#21262d' } },
            y: { ticks: { color: '#8b949e', callback: function(v) { return v.toLocaleString(); } }, grid: { color: '#21262d' } }
          }
        }
      });
    }
  })();
  </script>

  {% else %}
  <div style="text-align: center; padding: 60px; color: var(--text-secondary);">
    <p>No scenario data available.</p>
    <p style="font-size: 0.85rem;">Run BCBS 368 scenarios to enable the Scenario Studio.</p>
  </div>
  {% endif %}

===FILE START=== src/cockpit/pnl_dashboard/templates/_sensitivity.html
<div id="tab-sensitivity" class="tab-content">
  <h3 style="font-size: 0.9rem; margin-bottom: 12px;">Shock Sensitivity</h3>

  <!-- Toggle -->
  <div class="controls">
    <span style="color: var(--text-secondary); font-size: 0.8rem; line-height: 32px; margin-right: 8px;">Delta:</span>
    <button class="ctrl-btn active" onclick="setSensMode('50')">+50bp vs Base</button>
    <button class="ctrl-btn" onclick="setSensMode('wirp')">WIRP vs Base</button>
  </div>

  <div class="card">
    <div style="overflow-x: auto;">
      <table id="sensitivity-table">
        <thead id="sens-thead"></thead>
        <tbody id="sens-tbody"></tbody>
        <tfoot id="sens-tfoot"></tfoot>
      </table>
    </div>
  </div>

  <div class="card" style="text-align: center; padding: 12px;">
    <span style="font-size: 0.85rem; color: var(--text-secondary);">Grand Total NII Sensitivity: </span>
    <span id="sens-grand-total" style="font-size: 1.1rem; font-weight: 700;"></span>
  </div>

  <script>
  (function() {
    const sensData = {{ sensitivity | tojson_safe }};
    let sensMode = '50';

    function heatColor(val, maxAbs) {
      if (maxAbs === 0) return 'transparent';
      const ratio = Math.min(Math.abs(val) / maxAbs, 1);
      if (val > 0) return 'rgba(63, 185, 80, ' + (ratio * 0.5) + ')';
      if (val < 0) return 'rgba(248, 81, 73, ' + (ratio * 0.5) + ')';
      return 'transparent';
    }

    function renderSensTable() {
      const rows = sensMode === '50' ? sensData.rows_50 : sensData.rows_wirp;
      const totals = sensMode === '50' ? sensData.totals_50 : sensData.totals_wirp;
      const grandTotal = sensMode === '50' ? sensData.grand_total_50 : sensData.grand_total_wirp;
      const months = sensData.months || [];

      if (!rows || !rows.length || !months.length) {
        document.getElementById('sens-thead').innerHTML = '';
        document.getElementById('sens-tbody').innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="3" style="text-align:center; color: var(--text-secondary);">No sensitivity data available</td></tr>';
        document.getElementById('sens-tfoot').innerHTML = '';
        document.getElementById('sens-grand-total').textContent = '—';
        return;
      }

      // Find max absolute value for color scaling
      let maxAbs = 0;
      rows.forEach(r => r.values.forEach(v => { if (Math.abs(v) > maxAbs) maxAbs = Math.abs(v); }));

      // Header
      let thead = '<tr><th>Currency</th><th>Product</th>';
      months.forEach(m => { thead += '<th>' + m + '</th>'; });
      thead += '<th>Total</th></tr>';
      document.getElementById('sens-thead').innerHTML = thead;

      // Body
      let tbody = '';
      rows.forEach(r => {
        tbody += '<tr><td>' + r.currency + '</td><td>' + r.product + '</td>';
        r.values.forEach(v => {
          tbody += '<td style="background:' + heatColor(v, maxAbs) + '">' + fmt(v) + '</td>';
        });
        tbody += '<td style="font-weight:600;background:' + heatColor(r.total, maxAbs) + '">' + fmt(r.total) + '</td>';
        tbody += '</tr>';
      });
      document.getElementById('sens-tbody').innerHTML = tbody;

      // Currency total rows
      let tfoot = '';
      Object.keys(totals).sort().forEach(ccy => {
        const vals = totals[ccy];
        const total = vals.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0);
        tfoot += '<tr style="font-weight:600;background:var(--bg-tertiary);"><td>' + ccy + '</td><td>TOTAL</td>';
        vals.forEach(v => { tfoot += '<td>' + fmt(v) + '</td>'; });
        tfoot += '<td>' + fmt(total) + '</td></tr>';
      });
      document.getElementById('sens-tfoot').innerHTML = tfoot;

      // Grand total
      const gt = document.getElementById('sens-grand-total');
      gt.textContent = (grandTotal >= 0 ? '+' : '') + fmt(grandTotal);
      gt.className = valClass(grandTotal);
    }

    window.setSensMode = function(mode) {
      sensMode = mode;
      document.querySelectorAll('#tab-sensitivity .controls .ctrl-btn').forEach(b => {
        b.classList.toggle('active', (mode === '50' && b.textContent.includes('50')) || (mode === 'wirp' && b.textContent.includes('WIRP')));
      });
      renderSensTable();
    };

    renderSensTable();
  })();
  </script>
</div>

===FILE END=== src/cockpit/pnl_dashboard/templates/_sensitivity.html

    {{ kpi_card("Reserve Requirement", "{:,.0f}".format(snb_reserves.reserve_requirement), "", "2.5% of sight liabilities") }}
    {{ kpi_card("Eligible HQLA", "{:,.0f}".format(snb_reserves.eligible_hqla), "positive" if snb_reserves.eligible_hqla >= snb_reserves.reserve_requirement else "negative") }}
    {{ kpi_card("Coverage Ratio", "{:.1f}%".format(snb_reserves.coverage_pct), "positive" if snb_reserves.coverage_pct >= 100 else "negative") }}
    {{ kpi_card("Opportunity Cost", "{:,.0f}".format(snb_reserves.opportunity_cost), "negative" if snb_reserves.opportunity_cost > 0 else "neutral", "OIS × reserve excess") }}

  {% if snb_reserves.by_product %}

    <table>
      <thead>
        <tr>
          <th>Product</th>
          <th style="text-align:right;">Balance</th>
          <th style="text-align:right;">Reserve (2.5%)</th>
        </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
        {% for item in snb_reserves.by_product %}
        <tr>
          <td>{{ item.product }}</td>
          <td style="text-align:right;">{{ "{:,.0f}".format(item.balance) }}</td>
          <td style="text-align:right;">{{ "{:,.0f}".format(item.reserve) }}</td>
        </tr>
        {% endfor %}
      </tbody>
    </table>
  </div>
  {% endif %}

  <div class="card">
    <h3 style="font-size: 0.85rem; margin-bottom: 8px;">Reserve Waterfall</h3>
    <canvas id="snbReservesChart" height="280"></canvas>
  </div>

  <script>
  (function() {
    const data = {{ snb_reserves | tojson_safe }};
    if (!data) return;
    const labels = ['Sight Liabilities', 'Reserve Req (2.5%)', 'HQLA', 'Surplus/Deficit'];
    const vals = [
      data.total_sight_liabilities || 0,
      data.reserve_requirement || 0,
      data.eligible_hqla || 0,
      (data.eligible_hqla || 0) - (data.reserve_requirement || 0)
    ];
    const colors = vals.map((v, i) => i === 3 ? (v >= 0 ? '#3fb950' : '#f85149') : '#58a6ff');
    new Chart(document.getElementById('snbReservesChart'), {
      type: 'bar',
      data: { labels: labels, datasets: [{ data: vals, backgroundColor: colors, borderWidth: 0, borderRadius: 3 }] },
      options: {
        responsive: true,
        plugins: { legend: { display: false } },
        scales: {
          x: { grid: { display: false }, ticks: { color: '#e6edf3' } },
          y: { grid: { color: '#30363d' }, ticks: { color: '#8b949e' } }
        }
      }
    });
  })();
  </script>

  <p class="footnote">SNB minimum reserve per LiqV Art. 13: 2.5% of relevant CHF sight liabilities, computed on 20th of reporting month.</p>

  {% else %}
  {{ empty_state("No SNB reserve data available.", "Requires deal data with CHF sight deposit liabilities.") }}
  {% endif %}
</div>

            borderColor: '#0d1117',
            borderWidth: 2,
          }]
        },
        options: {
          responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false,
          plugins: { legend: { position: 'right', labels: { color: '#e6edf3', font: { size: 11 } } } }
        }
      });
    }

    // Waterfall chart
    if (typeof Chart !== 'undefined' && wf.labels && wf.labels.length) {
      new Chart(document.getElementById('chart-summary-waterfall'), {
        type: 'bar',
        data: {
          labels: wf.labels,
          datasets: [
            { label: 'Realized', data: wf.realized, backgroundColor: '#3fb950', stack: 's' },
            { label: 'Forecast', data: wf.forecast, backgroundColor: 'rgba(63,185,80,0.35)', stack: 's' },
          ]
        },
        options: {
          responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false,
          plugins: { legend: { labels: { color: '#e6edf3' } } },
          scales: {
            x: { stacked: true, ticks: { color: '#8b949e' } },
            y: { stacked: true, ticks: { color: '#8b949e' } }
          }
        }
      });
    }
  })();
  </script>

<div id="tab-trends" class="tab-content">
  <h3 style="font-size: 0.9rem; margin-bottom: 12px;">Historical Trends</h3>

  {% if has_trends %}

  <!-- Metric summary cards with sparklines -->
  <div style="display: grid; grid-template-columns: repeat(auto-fill, minmax(220px, 1fr)); gap: 12px; margin-bottom: 16px;">
    {% for name, m in trends.metrics.items() %}
    <div class="kpi-card" style="text-align: left; padding: 12px;">

        <span style="font-size: 0.7rem; padding: 2px 6px; border-radius: 3px;
          {% if m.trend == 'up' %}background: rgba(63,185,80,0.2); color: #3fb950;
          {% elif m.trend == 'down' %}background: rgba(248,81,73,0.2); color: #f85149;
          {% else %}background: rgba(139,148,158,0.2); color: #8b949e;{% endif %}">
          {% if m.trend == 'up' %}&#x25B2;{% elif m.trend == 'down' %}&#x25BC;{% else %}&#x25CF;{% endif %}
          {{ m.trend }}
        </span>
      </div>
      <div style="font-size: 1.25rem; font-weight: 700; margin: 4px 0;">
        {% if m.latest is not none %}{{ "{:,.2f}".format(m.latest) }}{% else %}&mdash;{% endif %}
      </div>
      <div style="font-size: 0.7rem; color: var(--text-secondary);">
        Range: {{ "{:,.2f}".format(m.min) }} &ndash; {{ "{:,.2f}".format(m.max) }} &middot;
        &sigma; {{ "{:,.2f}".format(m.std) }}
      </div>
      <canvas id="spark-{{ name }}" height="30" style="margin-top: 6px;"></canvas>
    </div>
    {% endfor %}
  </div>

  <!-- Main multi-line chart -->
  <div class="card" style="margin-bottom: 16px;">
    <h4 style="font-size: 0.85rem; margin-bottom: 8px;">KPI Time Series</h4>
    <div class="controls" id="trend-controls"></div>
    <div class="chart-container"><canvas id="chart-trends-main"></canvas></div>
  </div>

  <p class="footnote">
    Daily KPI snapshots saved automatically. Trends require at least 2 snapshots.
    Run <code>cockpit compute</code> daily to build history.
  </p>

  <script>
  (function() {
    const data = {{ trends | tojson_safe }};
    const dates = data.dates;
    const metricNames = Object.keys(data.metrics);
    const palette = ['#58a6ff', '#3fb950', '#d29922', '#f85149', '#e67e22', '#6f42c1', '#d62828', '#a5d6ff'];

    // Sparklines
    metricNames.forEach(function(name, idx) {
      var canvas = document.getElementById('spark-' + name);
      if (!canvas || typeof Chart === 'undefined') return;
      var values = data.metrics[name].values.filter(function(v) { return v !== null; });
      if (values.length < 2) return;
      new Chart(canvas, {
        type: 'line',
        data: {
          labels: values.map(function(_, i) { return i; }),
          datasets: [{
            data: values,
            borderColor: palette[idx % palette.length],
            backgroundColor: 'transparent',
            borderWidth: 1.5,
            pointRadius: 0,
            tension: 0.4,
          }]
        },
        options: {
          responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false,
          plugins: { legend: { display: false }, tooltip: { enabled: false } },
          scales: { x: { display: false }, y: { display: false } },
          animation: false,
        }
      });
    });

    // Main chart: all metrics on separate Y axes would be messy.
    // Instead: let user toggle which metrics to show.
    var mainChart = null;
    var activeMetrics = metricNames.slice(0, Math.min(3, metricNames.length));

    function renderMainChart() {
      var ctx = document.getElementById('chart-trends-main');
      if (!ctx || typeof Chart === 'undefined') return;
      if (mainChart) mainChart.destroy();

      var datasets = activeMetrics.map(function(name, idx) {
        return {
          label: name.replace(/_/g, ' '),
          data: data.metrics[name].values,
          borderColor: palette[idx % palette.length],
          backgroundColor: 'transparent',
          borderWidth: 2,
          pointRadius: 2,
          tension: 0.3,
          spanGaps: true,
        };
      });

      mainChart = new Chart(ctx, {
        type: 'line',
        data: { labels: dates, datasets: datasets },
        options: {
          responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false,
          interaction: { mode: 'index', intersect: false },
          plugins: { legend: { labels: { color: '#e6edf3', font: { size: 11 } } } },
          scales: {
            x: { ticks: { color: '#8b949e', maxRotation: 45, font: { size: 10 } } },
            y: { ticks: { color: '#8b949e' } }
          }
        }
      });
    }

    // Build toggle buttons
    var controlsEl = document.getElementById('trend-controls');
    metricNames.forEach(function(name, idx) {
      var btn = document.createElement('button');
      btn.className = 'ctrl-btn' + (activeMetrics.indexOf(name) >= 0 ? ' active' : '');
      btn.textContent = name.replace(/_/g, ' ');
      btn.style.borderLeftColor = palette[idx % palette.length];
      btn.style.borderLeftWidth = '3px';
      btn.onclick = function() {
        var i = activeMetrics.indexOf(name);
        if (i >= 0) { activeMetrics.splice(i, 1); btn.classList.remove('active'); }
        else { activeMetrics.push(name); btn.classList.add('active'); }
        renderMainChart();
      };
      controlsEl.appendChild(btn);
    });

    renderMainChart();
  })();
  </script>

  {% else %}
  <div style="text-align: center; padding: 60px; color: var(--text-secondary);">
    <p>No historical KPI data available.</p>
    <p style="font-size: 0.85rem;">Run <code>cockpit compute</code> daily to accumulate KPI snapshots in <code>data/kpi_snapshots/</code>.</p>
  </div>
  {% endif %}
</div>

<script>
function switchTab(id, evt) {
  document.querySelectorAll('.tab-content').forEach(el => el.classList.remove('active'));
  document.querySelectorAll('.tab-btn').forEach(el => el.classList.remove('active'));
  var tab = document.getElementById('tab-' + id);
  if (tab) tab.classList.add('active');
  var btn = (evt && evt.target) ? evt.target.closest('.tab-btn') : null;
  if (btn) btn.classList.add('active');
}
function fmt(n) {
  if (n == null || isNaN(n)) return '—';
  return Number(n).toLocaleString('en-US', {maximumFractionDigits: 0});
}
function fmtPct(n) {
  if (n == null || isNaN(n)) return '—';
  return Number(n).toFixed(4) + '%';
}
function valClass(n) { return n > 0 ? 'positive' : n < 0 ? 'negative' : 'neutral'; }

// CSV export for any table element
function exportTableCsv(tableEl, filename) {
  if (!tableEl) return;
  var csv = [];
  tableEl.querySelectorAll('tr').forEach(function(row) {
    var cols = [];
    row.querySelectorAll('th, td').forEach(function(cell) {
      var text = cell.innerText.replace(/"/g, '""').replace(/\s+/g, ' ').trim();
      cols.push('"' + text + '"');
    });
    csv.push(cols.join(','));
  });
  var blob = new Blob([csv.join('\n')], {type: 'text/csv;charset=utf-8;'});
  var link = document.createElement('a');
  link.href = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
  link.download = filename || 'export.csv';
  link.click();
}

// Add export buttons to all tables on load
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
  document.querySelectorAll('.tab-content table').forEach(function(tbl, idx) {
    var tabEl = tbl.closest('.tab-content');
    var tabName = tabEl ? tabEl.id.replace('tab-', '') : 'table';
    var btn = document.createElement('button');
    btn.className = 'ctrl-btn';
    btn.style.cssText = 'float: right; margin: 4px 0; font-size: 0.7rem; padding: 3px 8px;';
    btn.textContent = 'CSV';
    btn.title = 'Export table to CSV';
    btn.onclick = function() { exportTableCsv(tbl, tabName + '_' + idx + '.csv'); };
    tbl.parentElement.insertBefore(btn, tbl);
  });
});
</script>

</body>
</html>

===FILE START=== src/cockpit/render/charts.py
"""Chart data builders for cockpit HTML templates.

Each function takes raw data dicts (from JSON intermediates) and returns
structured dicts that Jinja2 templates embed as inline JSON for Chart.js.
"""

from __future__ import annotations

from cockpit.config import FX_ALERT_BANDS, SCENARIOS


def build_macro_charts(data: dict) -> dict:
    """Build data for Tab 1: Macro Overview.

    Returns dict with keys: score_cards, alerts, cb_rates, key_dates.
    """
    scores = data.get("scores", {})
    alerts = data.get("alerts", [])

    score_cards = {}
    for ccy in ("USD", "EUR", "CHF", "GBP"):
        s = scores.get(ccy, {})
        score_cards[ccy] = {
            "composite": s.get("composite", 0),
            "label": s.get("label", "N/A"),
            "driver": s.get("driver", ""),
            "families": s.get("families", {}),
        }

    cb_rates = {}
    rates = data.get("rates", {})
    if "fed_rates" in rates:
        cb_rates["Fed"] = {"rate": rates["fed_rates"].get("mid"), "name": "Fed Funds"}
    if "ecb_rates" in rates:
        cb_rates["ECB"] = {"rate": rates["ecb_rates"].get("deposit_facility"), "name": "Deposit Facility"}
    snb = rates.get("snb_rate")
    if snb is not None:
        cb_rates["BNS"] = {"rate": snb, "name": "Policy Rate"}

    return {
        "score_cards": score_cards,
        "alerts": alerts,
        "cb_rates": cb_rates,
        "key_dates": data.get("key_dates", []),
    }


def build_fx_energy_charts(data: dict) -> dict:
    """Build data for Tab 2: FX & Energy.

    Returns dict with keys: fx_series, energy_series, deltas, scenario_bands.
    """
    fx_series = {}
    for pair in ("usd_chf", "eur_chf", "gbp_chf"):
        history = data.get(f"{pair}_history", [])
        fx_series[pair] = {
            "dates": [p["date"] for p in history],
            "values": [p["value"] for p in history],
        }

    energy = data.get("energy", {})
    energy_series = {}
    for fuel in ("brent", "eu_gas"):
        history = energy.get(f"{fuel}_history", [])
        energy_series[fuel] = {
            "dates": [p["date"] for p in history],
            "values": [p["value"] for p in history],
        }

    return {
        "fx_series": fx_series,
        "energy_series": energy_series,
        "deltas": data.get("deltas", {}),
        "scenario_bands": SCENARIOS,
        "fx_bands": FX_ALERT_BANDS,
    }


def build_pnl_charts(data: dict) -> dict:
    """Build data for Tab 3: P&L Projection.

    Returns dict with keys: monthly_pnl, shock_comparison, book2_mtm, strategy_decomposition.
    """
    months = data.get("months", [])
    by_currency = data.get("by_currency", {})

    datasets = {}
    for ccy, shocks in by_currency.items():
        datasets[ccy] = {
            "shock_0": shocks.get("shock_0", []),
            "shock_50": shocks.get("shock_50", []),
            "shock_wirp": shocks.get("shock_wirp", []),
        }

    return {
        "monthly_pnl": {
            "labels": months,
            "datasets": datasets,
        },
        "shock_comparison": data.get("shock_comparison", {}),
        "book2_mtm": data.get("book2_mtm", []),
        "strategy_decomposition": data.get("strategy_decomposition", {}),
    }


def build_portfolio_charts(data: dict) -> dict:
    """Build data for Tab 4: Portfolio Snapshot.

    Returns dict with keys: liquidity_ladder, positions, concentration, rating, hqla.
    """
    exposure = data.get("exposure", {})
    buckets = exposure.get("buckets", [])

    liquidity_ladder = {
        "labels": [b["label"] for b in buckets],
        "inflows": [b["inflows"] for b in buckets],
        "outflows": [b["outflows"] for b in buckets],
        "net": [b["net"] for b in buckets],
        "cumulative": [b["cumulative"] for b in buckets],
        "survival_days": exposure.get("survival_days"),
    }

    positions = data.get("positions", {}).get("currencies", {})

    cpty = data.get("counterparty", {})
    concentration = cpty.get("concentration", {})
    rating = cpty.get("rating", {})
    hqla = cpty.get("hqla", {})

    return {
        "liquidity_ladder": liquidity_ladder,
        "positions": positions,
        "concentration": concentration,
        "rating": rating,
        "hqla": hqla,
    }

===FILE END=== src/cockpit/render/charts.py

===FILE START=== src/cockpit/render/renderer.py
"""Jinja2 renderer that assembles cockpit HTML from tab partials."""

from __future__ import annotations

import json
from pathlib import Path

from jinja2 import Environment, FileSystemLoader

from cockpit.render.charts import (
    build_macro_charts,
    build_fx_energy_charts,
    build_pnl_charts,
    build_portfolio_charts,
)

TEMPLATE_DIR = Path(__file__).parent / "templates"


def _json_filter(value: object) -> str:
    """Jinja2 filter to safely embed Python objects as inline JSON."""
    return json.dumps(value, default=str)


def render_cockpit(
    *,
    macro_data: dict | None,
    pnl_data: dict | None,
    portfolio_data: dict | None,
    scores_data: dict | None,
    brief_data: dict | None,
    date: str,
    output_path: Path,
) -> Path:
    """Render the cockpit HTML file from available data.

    Any data argument can be None — the template renders a placeholder for
    missing tabs instead of failing.

    Returns the output path.
    """
    env = Environment(
        loader=FileSystemLoader(str(TEMPLATE_DIR)),
        autoescape=False,
    )
    env.filters["tojson_safe"] = _json_filter

    # Build chart data from whatever is available
    macro_charts = build_macro_charts(macro_data or {})
    if scores_data:
        macro_charts["score_cards"] = {
            ccy: {
                "composite": s.get("composite", 0),
                "label": s.get("label", "N/A"),
                "driver": s.get("driver", ""),
                "families": s.get("families", {}),
            }
            for ccy, s in scores_data.items()
        }

    fx_energy_charts = build_fx_energy_charts(macro_data or {})
    pnl_charts = build_pnl_charts(pnl_data or {})
    portfolio_charts = build_portfolio_charts(portfolio_data or {})

    context = {
        "date": date,
        "has_macro": macro_data is not None,
        "has_pnl": pnl_data is not None,
        "has_portfolio": portfolio_data is not None,
        "has_brief": brief_data is not None,
        "macro": macro_charts,
        "fx_energy": fx_energy_charts,
        "pnl": pnl_charts,
        "portfolio": portfolio_charts,
        "brief": brief_data or {},
    }

    template = env.get_template("cockpit.html")
    html = template.render(**context)

    output_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    output_path.write_text(html, encoding="utf-8")
    return output_path

===FILE END=== src/cockpit/render/renderer.py

===FILE START=== src/cockpit/render/templates/_pnl.html
<div id="tab-pnl" class="tab-content">
  <div class="card" style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
    <h3 style="font-size: 0.9rem; margin-bottom: 8px;">Monthly P&amp;L by Currency (BOOK1)</h3>
    <div class="chart-container" style="height: 400px;">
      <canvas id="chart-monthly-pnl"></canvas>
    </div>
    <div style="margin-top: 8px; text-align: right;">
      <button onclick="togglePnlView()" style="background: var(--bg-tertiary); border: 1px solid var(--border); color: var(--text-primary); padding: 6px 12px; border-radius: 4px; cursor: pointer; font-size: 0.8rem;">
        Toggle Stacked / Side-by-Side
      </button>
    </div>
  </div>

  {% if pnl.book2_mtm %}
  <div class="card" style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
    <h3 style="font-size: 0.9rem; margin-bottom: 12px;">BOOK2 MTM — IRS Positions</h3>
    <table>
      <thead><tr><th>Deal</th><th>Currency</th><th>MTM</th></tr></thead>
      <tbody>
      {% for row in pnl.book2_mtm %}
        <tr><td>{{ row.deal }}</td><td>{{ row.currency }}</td><td>{{ "{:,.0f}".format(row.mtm) }}</td></tr>
      {% endfor %}
      </tbody>
    </table>
  </div>
  {% endif %}

  <script>
  let pnlStacked = true;
  const pnlData = {{ pnl.monthly_pnl | tojson_safe }};
  const colors = { CHF: '#d62828', EUR: '#e67e22', USD: '#002868', GBP: '#6f42c1' };
  let pnlChart = null;

  function renderPnlChart() {
    const ctx = document.getElementById('chart-monthly-pnl');
    if (!ctx || typeof Chart === 'undefined' || !pnlData.labels.length) return;
    if (pnlChart) pnlChart.destroy();
    const datasets = [];
    for (const [ccy, shocks] of Object.entries(pnlData.datasets)) {
      datasets.push({
        label: ccy + ' (base)',
        data: shocks.shock_0 || [],
        backgroundColor: colors[ccy] || '#58a6ff',
        stack: pnlStacked ? 'base' : ccy,
      });
    }
    pnlChart = new Chart(ctx, {
      type: 'bar',
      data: { labels: pnlData.labels, datasets },
      options: {
        responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false,
        plugins: { legend: { labels: { color: '#e6edf3' } } },
        scales: {
          x: { stacked: pnlStacked, ticks: { color: '#8b949e' } },
          y: { stacked: pnlStacked, ticks: { color: '#8b949e' } }
        }
      }
    });
  }
  function togglePnlView() { pnlStacked = !pnlStacked; renderPnlChart(); }
  renderPnlChart();
  </script>
</div>

===FILE END=== src/cockpit/render/templates/_pnl.html

  <script>
  (function() {
    const ladder = {{ portfolio.liquidity_ladder | tojson_safe }};
    const ctx = document.getElementById('chart-liquidity');
    if (ctx && typeof Chart !== 'undefined' && ladder.labels.length > 0) {
      new Chart(ctx, {
        type: 'bar',
        data: {
          labels: ladder.labels,
          datasets: [
            { label: 'Inflows', data: ladder.inflows, backgroundColor: 'rgba(63,185,80,0.7)' },
            { label: 'Outflows', data: ladder.outflows.map(v => -v), backgroundColor: 'rgba(248,81,73,0.7)' },
            { label: 'Cumulative', data: ladder.cumulative, type: 'line', borderColor: '#58a6ff', borderWidth: 2, pointRadius: 0, fill: false, yAxisID: 'y1' },
          ]
        },
        options: {
          responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false,
          plugins: { legend: { labels: { color: '#e6edf3' } } },
          scales: {
            x: { ticks: { color: '#8b949e', maxRotation: 45 } },
            y: { ticks: { color: '#8b949e' } },
            y1: { position: 'right', grid: { drawOnChartArea: false }, ticks: { color: '#58a6ff' } }
          }
        }
      });
    }

    const concData = {{ portfolio.concentration | tojson_safe }};
    const concCtx = document.getElementById('chart-concentration');
    if (concCtx && typeof Chart !== 'undefined' && concData.top_10 && concData.top_10.length > 0) {
      new Chart(concCtx, {
        type: 'doughnut',
        data: {
          labels: concData.top_10.map(c => c.counterparty),
          datasets: [{ data: concData.top_10.map(c => c.nominal), backgroundColor: ['#d62828','#e67e22','#002868','#6f42c1','#58a6ff','#3fb950','#d29922','#8b949e','#f0883e','#a5d6ff'] }]
        },
        options: {
          responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false,
          plugins: { legend: { position: 'right', labels: { color: '#e6edf3', font: { size: 10 } } } }
        }
      });
    }
  })();
  </script>
</div>

<script>
function switchTab(id) {
  document.querySelectorAll('.tab-content').forEach(el => el.classList.remove('active'));
  document.querySelectorAll('.tab-btn').forEach(el => el.classList.remove('active'));
  document.getElementById('tab-' + id).classList.add('active');
  event.target.classList.add('active');
}
</script>
